# <span data-ttu-id="05d42-104">JavaScript 版本信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="05d42-104">JavaScript version information</span></span>  

[!INCLUDE [deprecation-note](../../includes/legacy-edge-note.md)]  

<span data-ttu-id="05d42-105">JavaScript 支持因 Microsoft Edge、Microsoft Store 应用以及 Internet Explorer \ (IE\) 的不同文档模式而异。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="05d42-105">JavaScript support varies across Microsoft Edge, Microsoft Store apps, and different document modes of Internet Explorer \(IE\).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="05d42-106">有关 IE 文档代码版本处理的详细信息， [请参阅"定义文档兼容性](/previous-versions/windows/internet-explorer/ie-developer/compatibility/cc288325(v=vs.85))"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="05d42-106">For more information about IE document code versioning, see [Defining Document Compatibility](/previous-versions/windows/internet-explorer/ie-developer/compatibility/cc288325(v=vs.85)).</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="05d42-107">下表总结了所有设备、Microsoft Edge Internet Explorer和 Microsoft 应用商店应用中的 JavaScript 支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="05d42-107">The following table summarizes the JavaScript support across Internet Explorer, Microsoft Edge, and Microsoft Store apps.</span></span>  
  
> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="05d42-108">在某些情况下，应用商店应用支持 \ (从 \) 启用，在某些情况下 `about:flags` `Exp.` ，Windows 8 \ (v8\) 和 Windows 10 \ (v10\) 应用以及 Windows 桌面 \ (Win\) 和 Windows Phone \ (Phone\) （有所示）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="05d42-108">Experimental features \(enabled from `about:flags`\) are indicated by `Exp.` In some cases, Store apps support varies between Windows 8 \(v8\) and Windows 10 \(v10\) apps, and Windows desktop \(Win\) and Windows Phone \(Phone\), as indicated.</span></span>
